# WhisperRoom Quote Builder вҖ” Dev Log

Internal development notes. Last updated 2026-06-09.

> **Read this first when starting a session.** The "Current focus" section below is the fastest way to know where we left off. Below that: session writeups, the audit (outstanding work), and the changelog table.

## Current focus (2026-06-10 вҖ” Booth Builder real-component-art pass (v1.94.0): elevation now composites Benton's SketchUp renders of the actual parts; import pipeline + art manifest live. Before that v1.92.0 drawing-fidelity (VSS/EFS/roof-vent draw, true double wall) and v1.90.0 (customer-clean page). v1.84вҖ“1.90 on MAIN (`b334c86`).)

**Booth Builder (v1.92.0, staging):** Benton: "the new features don't actually populate anything" вҶ’ the ones that matter now DRAW, grounded in the customer drawings (catalog p.29 + `Applied Electronics` proposal back views + E spec sheets): **VSS** = two extra hose-connected silencer ducts on the vent wall (both views); **EFS** = floor silencer box wrapping the fan, protruding a true 10вҖі with the dim line flipping to "w/ EFS"; **Roof-mounted ventilation** (new toggle) = ducts ON the roof, vent wallвҶ’cable wall (same swap as the production RM BOM), nothing protrudes, EFS included. **Enhanced** booths now draw as the real thing вҖ” outer wall В· air gap В· full inner wall set w/ its own seam seals + corner posts (was one thick band). **Windows** are a bright full-thickness glass band you can visibly see through. Keys `ef`/`rv` ride payload+hash+server `safe`. Harnesses: `optspreview.js` (7 screenshot cases) + `wapreview.js`. bbtest 17/17. **Test on staging:** toggle VSS/EFS/roof on a 4872 (watch ducts + the w/-EFS dim), switch StandardвҶ”Enhanced (double wall), drop a window on an E booth. Summary-only still: Studio light / Cable jack panel / Bass traps / Office desk. Open: room-context mode, leader-line callouts, proposal-image export, quote-side `boothConfig` persistence.

**Booth Builder (v1.89.0, staging):** Benton reviewed the drawings we actually send clients (`Z:\Drawings and Proposals` proposal PDFs вҖ” SketchUp top-downs with the door drawn OPEN + swing arc, ft-in dims, room-context + vent/EFS callouts) and steered the builder toward them. Plus the standing Phase A remainder: quote-side `boothConfig` persistence + WA-Type readout on the quote.

### Session 2026-06-09 вҖ” what shipped
- **Top-Down Layout вҖ” full rebuild (v1.84.0 вҶ’ 1.84.20).** All 26 booth sizes digitized from the spec-sheet page-3 top-down views (was 3) via a parallel subagent pass; harness in `bot/specsheet-work/` (`render.py`, `gen-layouts.js`, `layout-render.js`, `splice.js`, `preview.js`, `mktest.js`). `booth-layouts.json` re-keyed by SIZE with per-variant `{wallThickness, interior}` + `module` + `door`; `boothLayout()` resolves S/E/SNV/ENV. Renderer (in `packing-list.html`, source-of-truth `layout-render.js`, kept in sync by `splice.js`): paneled walls, **drag-to-rearrange with a size constraint** (can't drop a 46вҖі in a 22вҖі slot) + drag ghost, side-aware vent ducts + outward door that follow a dragged panel to any wall, exterior+interior dim lines. Vents scale with the wall (big on 46вҖі). **Seam seals** = subtle foam-comb lining + bold connectors: `midSeal()` plinth (base + centered tab) at panel joints, `cornerSeal()` chamfered L at corners (modeled off Benton's diagram). 127-LP pentagon still unsupported.
- **PL BOM accuracy:** RM adds **EFS per vent set** (1.84.5) + **ceiling support beam** (U101/U01 per D101/D12) on Standard booths (1.84.10). **Multi-booth accessory split** вҖ” qty-N booth line divides accessory qtys by N (1.84.8, fixed 12-bass-traps-on-every-booth). PL reads **foam/hinge/WA-type off the order**, not just the quote (1.84.12). **HX + WA/ADA EXT-wall re-size** (1.84.24) per the spec chart (`hx_wa_ext_swap` in feature-rules.json, keyed by WA Type), incl. the 4016 **tall jamb adapter Z19вҶ’Z20/Z21** (1.84.25) + a **per-booth Door-jamb toggle** on the PL (1.84.26).
- **Weights tool:** new **Studio Lights tab** (`/api/weights-sl`) вҖ” per size: vent sets, SL composition, summed SL weight vs the `SL <size>` SKU; first col = SL SKU for VLOOKUP (1.84.15/.18). **WA UPG host fix** in the Package Audit (1.84.14) вҖ” 40вҖівҶ’6084, 46вҖівҶ’7296, STD/ENHвҶ’S/E.
- **рҹ”Ҙ Price-book incident (1.84.22).** Benton's CSV product re-import changed HubSpot product **record IDs**; saved quotes store the old `productId`, so loading them showed wild "price changed" prompts. Fix: `/api/check-prices` matches by **name** now, not the stored ID. Restart/cache was NOT the cause вҖ” the data IDs moved. **Follow-ups:** re-run that import matched on Record ID; optional one-time migration to re-map old quotes' `productId`s by name.
- **Misc:** Shipping-labels page favicon (1.84.13).

**Active PL feature work (2026-06-08):**
- **HX / CP / SL вҖ” DONE (v1.73.0).** Rules in `lib/packing-list.js` + new `lib/pl-data/feature-rules.json`, derived from the 52 HX+CP+SL reference PLs (`WR PO System/PL Files/PLsFeatures`, diffed vs Base PLs) and verified end-to-end (`generate()` reconstructs all 52 exactly, components + weight). NV variants map SNVвҶ’S / ENVвҶ’E; HX hardware swap built generically from `HDWR <model>` packs (all four variants). The reusable diff/oracle harness lives in `WR PO System/PL Files/` (`feature_diff.py`, `build_feature_rules.py`, `verify_generator.js`).
- **ADA вҖ” DONE (v1.74.0).** Per-model `ada_by_model` rule derived from the 16-PL `PLsADA` batch (diffed vs base, oracle 14/14). ADA door is its OWN SKU set (Z30 frame / Z32 door / Z38 adaptor; inner Z34/Z35), distinct from the standalone WA-UPG door вҖ” so ADA is its own `^ADA` rule, not a reuse of the WA rule. Elevated-floor codes now known: Z40 cnr + Z42/Z43 ctr + Z44/Z45/Z46 side + perimeter Z48вҖ“Z55 (std-only). Open follow-ups: (1) **L-hinge ADA door** (need the Z31/Z33 L-variant codes вҖ” batch is R only); (2) **7296 4646 variant** (batch defaulted to 4622; force 4646 if a quote needs the alt door placement); (3) **Elevated Floor / Ramp as standalone features** (user said EF can be ordered separately, requires WA вҖ” currently only via ADA). Geometry reference: memory `project_wa_ada_door_geometry`.
- **Orders drawer (decisions locked 2026-06-08).**
  - вң… **DONE (v1.75.0):** PL link at the top of the `/orders` drawer (`#packingListBtn` вҶ’ `/pl/:quote`, new tab); box count + hardware box # auto-fill from the PL (`generate()` totals.boxCount/hardwareBox; `autofillFromPackingList()` seeds blank `#editBoxes`/`#editHardwareBox`).
  - вң… **DONE (v1.78.0) вҖ” two-way S/N sync.** `/api/packing-list/:quote` now returns `order_data.serialNumber`; PL viewer seeds each booth's S/N from line `ri` and debounce-saves via `PATCH /api/orders/:q` with `{serialNumber}` (reuses the drawer Save-Changes path вҖ” merges order_data + mirrors HubSpot `description`; QB stays at-ship). Dropped the localStorage S/N. Booth `ri` вҶ” line `ri`; with v1.77.0 expansion, each line = one physical booth.
  - вҸі **Small remaining bug:** `hardware_box` is written `parseInt()` at quote-server.js:14198 / :10928 but the value is free text ("Box 17") вҶ’ coerces to 0 in HubSpot; make it a string consistently (it's already `String(...)` at :13950).

**State of play:**
- **PL viewer redesigned** to match the real printed PL: centered WR logo + "Sound Isolation Enclosures" tagline, editable date, deal-ref header, MDL line w/ feature normalizer (`EFS / VSS / WDO 3236 / DESK / ADA`), Totals box (Cubic Feet / Pounds / Cubic Meters / Kilograms), big **PACKING LIST** title + editable **S/N** input (`localStorage`-persisted per-quote), per-booth one-page layout (page-break on print). Each PL row = ONE physical item (BOM qty=N expands to N rows). Columns: `# | L (in/m) | W (in/m) | T (in/m) | Weight (lb/kg) | Code | Part # | Package Contents`. (v1.72.6 / 1.72.7).
- **Feature substitution rules live** (`lib/packing-list.js` `FEATURE_SUBS` array + `applyFeatureSubs(features, ctx)` w/ `resolve()` callback for swap-style rules):
  - **VSS / EFS** вҖ” sized вҶ’ per vent set (booth's F01 qty), bare вҶ’ 1 (1.72.9)
  - **MJP** вҖ” constant +F09 (excl. ADPT/EXT) (1.72.10)
  - **DESK** вҖ” `Office Desk S` вҶ’ S02, `Office Desk L` вҶ’ S03 (1.72.10)
  - **WDO** вҖ” swap std wall for window wall + inner-shell K-family on E/ENV (TOP+BOT for big windows, SINGLE for smallest in each family) (1.72.11 / 1.72.12)
  - **WA Door** вҖ” swap STD door/frame for Z03вҖ“Z06 + Z25 (40"-wall) or Z120 (46"-wall) adapter + inner shell on E/ENV (handles both M01/L01 and K114/K116 inner-door families). **Plus narrow-wall shrink:** 46" booths C111 STDWL22 вҶ’ C112 STDWL19 (3" shrink, K112 вҶ’ K113 inner); 40" booths C10 STDWL16 вҶ’ Z02 STDWL7/WL16 bundle (49+7 conserves vs 40+16 = 56"). (1.72.15 / 1.72.28 / 1.72.30)
  - **STEP** вҖ” +S01 (1.72.17)

- **Config-driven swaps** (post-feature-subs in `generate()`, both **now pulled from the quote snap** in `/api/packing-list` вҖ” `snap.acceptedHinge` / `snap.repHingePreference`, `snap.acceptedFoam` / `snap.repFoamColor`; "Left Hand"/"Right Hand" normalized to "Left"/"Right"; foam values 1:1 to FOAM_OPTIONS):

- **Top-Down Layout tab** (1.72.25 вҶ’ 1.72.33). Each PL block gets a рҹ“Ұ Packing List В· рҹҸ— Top-Down Layout tab pair (print forces PL). Layouts live in `lib/pl-data/booth-layouts.json` вҖ” slot schema is `{id, size, families[], prefers[]}` keyed by wall side N/S/E/W. `lib/packing-list.js` `boothLayout(name)` does exact match + variant fallback (4872 E вҶ’ 4872 S layout), and `generate()` ships only the layouts referenced by the current quote. Frontend `placeBom()` walks slots greedily, accepting any pack in `slot.families` (so the WA shrink C111вҶ’C112 lands cleanly + the WA STDDRFRM lands in the door slot); `panelInteriorWidth()` renders Z03 at 49вҖі, C112 at 19вҖі, Z02 at 7вҖі in the SVG. **3 booths digitized so far:** MDL 4242 S (44Г—44 square, 4Г—40вҖі), MDL 4848 S (50Г—50 square, 4Г—46вҖі), MDL 4872 S (74Г—50 rect, 46+22 long sides). All inherit to E variants via fallback. **22 unique shapes remain** вҖ” all PDFs available at `C:\Users\bento\OneDrive\Documents\Claude\WhisperRoom PL\TopDowns\`. Rectangular shapes need BOM reconciliation pass (e.g. 4260 S has 5 walls for a 40Г—58 interior that *looks* like it wants 6 slots).
- **MDL title normalizer** in `packing-list.html` вҖ” strips booth size/variant from quote feature names (`EFS 4872` вҶ’ `EFS`); keeps window size on `WDO 3236 S` вҶ’ `WDO 3236`; maps `Office Desk S/L` вҶ’ `DESK`; drops internal hardware (HEPA/HX/AP/CP/EFP/etc.) from the MDL title. Dedupes. Customer-facing tokens only.
- **`/assets/whisperroom-logo.svg` endpoint** added вҖ” `quote-server.js` serves the existing `assets/whisperroom-logo.svg.b64` decoded.

**Pre-commit hook (1.72.14):** `scripts/check-syntax.js` runs `node --check` on every staged JS file + `require`+invoke smoke-test on `templates/changelog.js` and `lib/packing-list.js` (the two files that crash the server at startup if they fail to load). Tracked at `scripts/git-hooks/pre-commit` w/ one-shot installer `scripts/install-hooks.sh`. Birthed by v1.72.11's prod crash: an over-escaped apostrophe in a changelog entry threw `SyntaxError: Unexpected identifier 's'` at server startup; both staging and prod crash-looped before v1.72.13 hotfix. The hook **earned its keep on the very next commit (v1.72.16) вҖ” caught me repeating the exact same mistake** while writing the hinge-swap changelog entry. `/bump` slash command and `CLAUDE.md` updated to document the workflow + the apostrophe gotcha.

**Weight reconciliation against the quote (verification oracle, Benton):**
- **ОЈ of all PL totals across all booths Г— room.qty should equal the quote's weight** вҖ” that's the gold-standard cross-check.
- Today PL = **net** (ОЈ component lb); quote freight = **gross** (net + pallets via `PALLETS_PER_MDL Г— 144`). They're off by pallet weight per booth. Either: (a) add a Gross line to the PL totals using the same pallet-count map, OR (b) compare to a net-only number the quote exposes (the `/weights` page already computes ОЈ rounded components per MDL).
- **No multi-booth grand total exists** yet вҖ” each PL page has its own totals box, but there's no "all booths combined" stat to diff against the quote. Quick add: sum `roomNet * room.qty` across rooms and render in the page footer (or on the first page).
- Same-MDL qty>1 quote lines also affect this: current PL multiplies by `room.qty` in the totals math but the table shows single-booth rows; the math should still tie out at the totals level, but the layout question (1 page w/ Г—N badge vs N pages each w/ own S/N) is separate from the totals reconciliation.

**Open verification items on already-shipped rules:**
- **WA Door 40вҖі inner shell** вҖ” outer C10 вҶ’ Z02 wired but no IEP bundle equivalent exists; K09 IEPWL11.5 stays put on E/ENV. Confirm against a real 40вҖі+WA+ENH PL.
- **RM on SNV/ENV** вҖ” do `VNT NV` walls also flip to CBL? Skipped; no `CBL NV` exists.
- **STDWL16 / IEPWL11.5 with RM** вҖ” no `CBL` variant; lines stay VNT. Real data gap or intentional?
- **WDO `43"` cases on 7296** вҖ” quote uses `WDO 43" 2636 S` but BOM has no `STDWL43`; stays unmapped (likely ADA-modified config вҖ” verify with example).
- **Default hinge** is `'Left'` in `DEFAULTS` but base BOM is R-default. Is L actually the production default, or should DEFAULTS flip? (Now mostly moot since quote's hinge wins; matters only when neither acceptedHinge nor repHingePreference is set.)
- **Layout: window placement** вҖ” `WDO 3236` window-wall (C104) lands on whichever STDWL46 slot is free since no slot has `WDO` in `prefers`. Read-only OK; revisit in the Phase-2 drag-to-swap pass.

**Open ideas (Benton, 2026-06-07):**
- **Seam seals in the layout** вҖ” Benton flagged: two kinds in the BOM (corner `D01 STDSS CNR` / `N01 IEPSS CNR` = 4 pieces per pack at the 4 booth corners; mid-wall `D02 STDSS MID` / `O01 IEPSS MID` = "T"-pieces joining two parallel panels on the same wall). Visualization plan: draw small black corner glyphs at each of the 4 interior corners of the booth (matches what the spec-sheet diagrams already show), plus a thin dark "T" mark at every adjacency between two slots on the same wall (e.g. between N-wide and N-narrow on 4872 S). Counts already reconcile: 4242 S (no multi-panel walls) has D01Г—1 + 0Г— D02; 4872 S (2 multi-panel long walls) has D01Г—1 + D02Г—1 (1 pack = 2 mids). Defer to Phase 2; this is purely visual, no PL/BOM math change.
- **Layout Phase 2 вҖ” drag-to-swap.** SVG slots become drop targets; dragging a placed panel to another compatible slot re-runs `placeBom()` with a forced assignment and re-renders. Then **Phase 3 вҖ” anomaly detection** (BOM has 2 vent walls but only 1 slot accepts vent, etc.).
- **PDF export of the PL** via Puppeteer (`lib/pdf.js` shared semaphore pattern, mirror the vendor-PO approach).
- **S/N persistence in Postgres** on the order record (today `localStorage` per-browser).

**State of play** (full detail in the 2026-06-05 session writeup below):
- **Packing List generator вҖ” Phase 1 spine LIVE** (v1.69.0). Quote вҶ’ rooms (each `MDLвҖҰ` line = a booth, following lines = its features) вҶ’ booth base BOM вҶ’ `/pl/:quoteNumber` viewer ("View Packing List" button in builder). Booth BOM is exact (weights tie out); **optional features are detected but flagged, NOT yet substituted.**
- **PL data foundation done & reconciled:** `lib/pl-data/` = `base-bom.json` (104) + `components-master.json` (1036 parts; **104/104 BOMs reconcile, 0 weight mismatch**) + `pallet-dims.json` (104). Source artifacts live in `WR PO System\PL Files\`.

### Packing List migration вҖ” NEW major initiative (scoped 2026-06-04)
Replacing the ~18MB `PackingList.xlsm` (Excel/VBA: 43 sheets, ~112K chars VBA, CSV-synced to a pCloud `Z:\` share) with a web module here: **packing-list generator + inventory + shipping/allocation + (future) barcode pack-verification.** Full scope in **`PACKING_LIST_SCOPE.md`** (repo root); project memory `project_packing_list_migration.md`.

**Architecture decided with Benton:**
- **Generate FROM the deal/order** (pre-fill model+features, rep confirms, manual overrides kept). Auto weight-check vs the quote's weight.
- **Generator = base BOM + ordered substitution ops** (REPLACE/ADD/REMOVE), code-level + feature-gated; combos as multi-condition rules. Replaces the per-cell `=IF()` matrix + `Calculations!AB` override hack with one inspectable pipeline.
- **Taxonomy:** ~26 sizes Г— {S, E, SNV, ENV} = **104 base BOMs.** E = S + inner IEP shell; NV = S/E minus ventilation (swap `вҖҰVNT` walls вҶ’ NV, drop Vent Set + fan unit). S/E = most of sales.
- **Constraint layer** (separate from swaps; drives configurator gray-out + generator guard): NV вҶ’ no vent add-ons (RM/VSS/EFS/HEPA); ADA only on a handful of models (extract from `Sheet1!AM2:AO100`); WA needs вүҘ60" in one dimension; RM has a min size. Mine the full matrix from the workbook вҶ’ Benton confirms.
- **Inventory/shipping** вҶ’ Postgres, transactional (kills the CSV last-writer-wins drift); allocation reserves, ship deducts atomically, audit log. **No pricing** (quote-side only). Fishbowl `Export1` is dead. Single on-hand per component.
- **Barcode** = future phase, designed-for: existing component labels just get a barcode of the component code; prototype camera-first on a phone (no scanner needed).
- **Reuse** the vendor-PO pattern: `/pl/:num?t=token` page вҶ’ Puppeteer PDF вҶ’ dual Drive drop (order + client folder) вҶ’ share link; new `/packing` dashboard.

**Two verification oracles:** (1) the workbook's golden weights (regenerate every model, compare summed weight); (2) Benton's real example PLs (5 in `WR PO System\PL Files\PL Examples\`).

**In flight now:** Benton running `BatchGenerateBasePLs` (VBA harness in `WR PO System\PL Files\BatchGenerateBasePLs.vba`) to emit all 104 base PLs into a `Base PLs\` folder. Diffing **SвҶ”E** (Enhancement/inner-shell delta) and **SвҶ”SNV** (No-Vent rule) from that output auto-derives those two structural rules. Extraction support: `WR PO System\PL Files\extract_pl.py` вҶ’ `_extract\` (VBA + sheet TSVs).

**Next:** when the 104-PDF batch finishes вҶ’ **Phase 0**: extract base BOMs + substitution rules + constraint matrix from `StandardModels`/`Parts`/`ADAInfo`; verify against both oracles.

Two new `/api/marketing/drill` types (router.js): **`paid-unattributed`** = paid closed-won deals (closed in window, `contactPaid`) where `NOT EXISTS` a `campMatch` to any current campaign (same `is_closed_won` + `closed_at` + contact-date windows as the headline `deals_won_selected` and as `campaign-attribution`, so the popup count == the row's number); **`paid-unattributed-term`** = same but `NOT EXISTS` a `termMatch` to any synced search term (mirrors `search-term-attribution`). - **v1.82.4** (Gabe) вҖ” **Deploy 3: Search-Term Mining (Growth Engine В§в‘Ҙ).** New frontend-only section that mines `marketing_search_terms` (+ `/search-term-attribution` for HubSpot revenue/term) against `marketing_keywords` (match_type) and GSC organic rankings. `gscBuildSearchTermMining(stRows, stAttrRows, kwRows, queries)` aggregates terms by normalized text, merges revenue, and produces four review queues: **(1) Negatives** вҖ” `cost вүҘ ST_MIN_SPEND($40)` + 0 conversions + $0 revenue + not branded; reason-tagged via `gscTermNegReason` (Competitor brand / Off-productВ·DIYВ·info / Spend-no-conv) using editable `GSC_COMPETITOR_TOKENS` + `GSC_NEGATIVE_TOKENS`. **(2) Harvest** вҖ” converting/revenue terms (`revWon>0 || conversionsвүҘ1`) not already in the keyword set, not branded; sorted by revenue then conversions. **(3) Cannibalization** вҖ” paid terms where our best GSC organic position вүӨ `ST_CANN_MAXPOS(3.5)` (we already rank top-3 free); brand-flagged. **(4) Match-type tightening** вҖ” Phrase/Broad keywords (`gscMatchLabel` maps enum 2/3/4 + string names) with `cost вүҘ $40` and (0 conv OR CPA > `ST_MT_CPA_MAX($250)`). `renderGrowthMining` draws a 4-panel responsive grid (`.mine-*` CSS), each capped at top 15 with an explicit "+N more" note (no silent truncation). Wired into `loadGrowthTab` (two new fetches: `/search-terms` + `/search-term-attribution`). All thresholds + token lists are Gabe-editable consts. Each panel is framed as a REVIEW queue, not an auto-action вҖ” $0 attributed revenue can be a real miss or an attribution gap (same caveat as the budget board). **Match-type #4 turned out fully buildable** (keywords carry `match_type`), so no ETL change was needed. Needs Sync All for full signal. Staging-only.
- **v1.82.2** (Gabe) вҖ” **Growth Engine accuracy pass (pre-Deploy-3).** (Renumbered from a draft v1.72.4 to stay on the single repo-wide sequence вҖ” v1.72.4 was already Benton's pallet-reduction batch.) Verified the rebuilt board's math against the live synced output before acting on it; fixed three distortions in `gscBuildPaidGrowth`/`gscBuildGrowthModel`/`renderGrowthExec`. **(1) $0-CRM-revenue campaigns no longer mislabeled "Maintain вҖ” steady performer."** Root cause: the old `noRev` gate required `conversions < 1`, so any campaign with Google conversions but $0 HubSpot revenue (LP General $8,898, Telehealth, Voice Over A/B) failed every branch and fell through to `else вҶ’ maintain`, and the v1.72.3 `investigate` bucket sat empty because its gate was too strict (even Shopify, an ecom-named campaign, landed in Maintain). Replaced `noRev` with `noCrmRev` (`cost вүҘ 300 && revenue вүӨ 0`) + `hasGoogleConv` (`conversions вүҘ 1`); now `noCrmRev && (attrGap || hasGoogleConv)` вҶ’ **investigate** ("conversions aren't tying back to CRM вҖ” check attribution/lead quality"), `noCrmRev` with no conversions вҶ’ **pause**. Opportunity-card mirror updated to match (Attribution Gap card checked before the savings/Low-ROAS catch). `maintain` now only catches genuinely-positive ROAS. **(2) `maxRev` normalizer no longer contaminated by Ignored queries** вҖ” a high-volume informational query ("how to choose a record player," ~$94k modeled) was setting `maxRev` and squashing every real Growth Score's revenue component; now normalizes only over `scoreable` opps (mirrors the Ignore gate: drops `informational` + `seo` with `commercialIntent < 25`). **(3) Exec header honesty** вҖ” "If you do 5 things this month / ~$102,381" implied the 5 listed actions delivered $102k, but that figure summed all ~38 ranked opps (the 5 shown sum to ~$32k, and overlap on shared pages). Header вҶ’ "Your top 5 moves right now"; subtitle now splits "These 5: ~$X modeled upside" from "full ranked list (N): ~$Y upside + ~$Z savings." Also clarified SEO `revenue_opportunity` is modeled upside (impr Г— CTR-gap Г— rev/click), not measured revenue. Frontend-only, `marketing-dashboard.html`. **Deploy 3 (search-term mining) still next.** Staging-only.

- **v1.71.2** (Gabe) вҖ” **Commercial Page Mapping Layer** вҖ” fixes the "ideal page = /products/drum-booth for everything" bug. ROOT CAUSE: `gscMatchCommercialPage` scored token overlap, but "booth" is a token in ~every commercial URL, so every booth query tied at overlap=1 and the click tie-break picked the highest-traffic booth page (drum-booth). New `gscPageKind` (product/application/category/package/home/blog/other); `gscPageClass` refactored on top of it; `gscPageKindChip` shown in ranking-page cells, action cards, Target Page Analysis. `gscPageMatchStatus(actualPage, idealPath)` shared by `gscDiagnose` + `gscMatchStatus` вҖ” actual===ideal вҶ’ **correct** (then CTR/Ranking/Content/Authority diagnosis, no longer forced wrong-page). `gscMatchCommercialPage` removed. All three GSC tables (overlap/queries/pages) are **sortable + paginated** (50/page, all rows) via `gscPaint()`; Organic Pages has a **Hide /blog** toggle. **Organic Leads + Closed Rev cards drillable** вҶ’ new `organic-leads`/`organic-revenue` drill types (HubSpot contacts/deals). Sync GSC honors the selected range (14вҖ“365d). Staging-only.
- **v1.65.2** (Gabe) вҖ” **GSC sync hardening + disk-capacity guard (post-incident).** A v1.65.1 365-day Sync All hit the uncapped/un-batched GSC step and **filled the shared Postgres volume to 98%, briefly taking the whole app down** (volume since grown 0.5GBвҶ’5GB). Fixes: (1) **pre-sync `_capacityCheck`** in router вҖ” `pg_database_size` vs `PG_SOFT_LIMIT_MB` (default 4500) вҶ’ returns **507 + clear message** if near-full instead of crashing the disk; (2) GSC upsert **batched** (~500 rows/statement) вҖ” row-by-row over 100k+ daily rows was the perf killer; (3) dedicated **"Sync GSC" button** (bounded to the visible date range) + GSC line in the status bar; (4) `all` sync caps GSC at **120d**. **LESSON: every data sync must guard against exceeding Postgres volume before pulling** вҖ” daily-granularity ETLs can balloon a shared DB fast. Staging-only.
- **v1.65.1** (Gabe) вҖ” **Marketing dashboard tabbed: Google Ad Spend + new Google Search Console.** New `marketing/gsc-etl.js` pulls organic Search Analytics (queries + pages) through our own Google OAuth (refresh token now carries the `webmasters.readonly` scope); `marketing_gsc_queries`/`_pages` tables; router gains `gsc` sync + `/gsc-queries|pages|overlap|summary` endpoints. GSC tab = organic KPI strip (tied to HubSpot ORGANIC_SEARCH leads/revenue at channel level) + **PaidГ—Organic Overlap** (cannibalization vs organic-gap tagging) + top queries/pages. QueryвҶ’deal organic attribution is impossible (Google withholds the organic term) вҖ” revenue ties channel-level only. Reuses GOOGLE_ADS_* creds + GSC_SITE_URL. Staging-only.
- **v1.65.0** (Benton) вҖ” **Accountant Payouts Portal** at `/portal/payouts`: password-gated public page exposing the exact HubSpot Payouts view to the outside accountant, walled off from the rest of the app. Env-only password (`ACCOUNTANT_PORTAL_PASSWORD`) вҖ” **must be set in Railway (staging + prod) or the portal 503s.** Pushed to staging; promote not yet requested.
- **v1.64.0** (Benton) вҖ” **Sales by State вҶ’ fiscal year (NovвҖ“Oct) + Income-tax nexus column.** Report rebucketed from calendar to fiscal years (FY2024/FY2025 = two most recent complete FYs); new income-tax economic-nexus column (`INCOME_NEXUS` in `lib/states.js`). Promoted to main 2026-06-03.
- **v1.63.0вҖ“v1.63.1** (Benton) вҖ” **HubSpot Payouts tab on `/accounting`** (groups succeeded payments by `hs_payout_date`; each group = one bank deposit, expandable to member payments) + the "Invalid time value" parser hotfix. New endpoint `GET /api/accounting/hubspot-payouts`. _(Promoted to main 2026-06-03.)_
- **v1.61.3** (Gabe) вҖ” Hotfix: three `SELECT DISTINCT` drill queries from v1.61.2 (term-deals, term-closed, segment-revenue) 500'd with "ORDER BY expressions must appear in select list" вҖ” now sort by the `amount` output alias. Staging-only.
- **v1.61.2** (Gabe) вҖ” **Marketing dashboard drill-downs + segment reclassification.** Share-of-closed-revenue and ad-acquisition-quality pills now open popups of the closed-won deals behind them; search-term **Leads / Deals / True ROAS** cells open the attributed contacts / deals / closed-won deals. Extends `GET /api/marketing/drill` (ad-quality, segment-revenue, term-leads/deals/closed), each reusing its source number's join+window so counts reconcile. Segment map: Testing-CombinedвҶ’Audiology, new **Competitors** segment, Unclassified bundled into **Mixed**. Staging-only.

Floor (first+latest touch only). New endpoint `GET /api/marketing/ad-quality`; `BRAND_TERMS` is Gabe-eyeball config. Staging-only.
- **v1.59.4** (Gabe) вҖ” **Marketing dashboard drill-down popups** (click HubSpot Contacts / Closed Revenue cards + funnel Quotes/Closed/Revenue вҶ’ modal listing the actual contacts/deals, each linking to its HubSpot record), bundled with the **funnel maturity bar** and the **"why these differ from HubSpot вҖә Ads"** notes panel. Staging-only per the marketing-dashboard rule. ### Today's session вҖ” WR PO System rollout

Today shipped **Phases 2 and 3** of the WR PO System end-to-end. Heavy iteration on the `/vpo/` doc page based on Benton testing the flow as we went:

- **Phase 2 (v1.50.0вҖ“v1.50.7):** Receive workflow вҖ” purple Receive button on `/vpo/` + Vendor Hub rows, modal with per-line ordered / received / remaining / receiving-now (default = remaining for one-click "receive everything"), receipt log on `/vpo/` (auth-only), button label flips to "Receipts" when RECEIVED. Big design decision mid-session: **the PDF is now a snapshot of what was sent, not a live document.** Stripped auto-PDF-regen from POST / PATCH / receive; PDF only updates when Josh explicitly hits "Update PO" (formerly Create / Download PDF вҖ” label flips after first generation, confirm dialog before replacing). Vendor Hub gained inline Send / Receive / Delete / Г— buttons; Send stays visible after status flips to SENT so Josh can reopen the draft if the mail client closed.
- **Phase 3 (v1.51.0):** Kim's invoice matching вҖ” new **Vendor Bills** tab on `/accounting` listing every PO that needs (or has) a vendor invoice matched. Two actions per row: **Open in QB** (opens blank `/app/bill?txnId=-1` New Bill page; QB Online doesn't support URL pre-fill so Kim picks vendor manually вҖ” Phase 4 would API-stub-create) + **Mark Bill Received** (modal: invoice # / date / total / QB Bill # / notes with live discrepancy banner). On save, appends to `invoice_data.events`, sums totals, flips status to **CLOSED** when fully received AND fully invoiced (Вұ$0.01), stamps `closed_at`. Partial bills supported natively (array of events, mirrors `received_data`).
- **Bonus:** the Sales Goal report on `/reports` got a "View deals counted" expandable list so reps can eyeball which deals are/aren't being counted toward MTD (with an explicit note that refunds aren't included).

### Open follow-ups вҖ” WR PO System

- **Phase 4: QB Bill auto-create.** Skip-aheaded today; ship when Kim asks. Build a `createQbBill()` wrapper in `lib/quickbooks.js` (first AP code вҖ” all existing exports are sales/AR), add `qb_vendor_id` column to `vendors`, on "Open in QB" POST a stub Bill (vendor + total + single Materials line) and deep-link to `/app/bill?txnId=<id>` so Kim opens a partially-created Bill to edit lines + attach PDF. Decision rationale: ship Phase 3 manual-flow first, watch Kim use it, design Phase 4 against real friction points.

### Decisions captured this week (2026-05-28 to 2026-05-29)

- **Audimute stays separate** вҖ” sales-rep drop-ship system, not supply-chain. Lives in its own `supplier_pos` table and `/suppliers` page.
- **PO prefix changed mid-flight** from `WV-` to `WP-` ("WhisperRoom Purchase") on 2026-05-29; existing WV-вҖҰ POs stay as-is (no migration).
- **Mailto with manual PDF attach** is the canonical send pattern (mailto can't carry attachments). Send body dropped the `/vpo/` link since Josh always attaches the PDF.
- **PDF lifecycle**: PDF is the snapshot we sent vendor. `/vpo/` URL is the live internal resource (with receipt log, edit affordances). Only the explicit "Update PO" button regenerates the Drive PDF.
- **Vendor info edits auto-propagate** to the vendor record (no confirm prompt) so the next PO inherits the latest info. Only catalog *price* changes prompt before propagating.
- **Refunds invisible to sales-goal calc** (per Benton 2026-05-29) вҖ” reconcile remains the source of truth for refund tracking.

## Earlier focus (2026-05-22 вҖ” Quote expiration indicators + marketing dashboard handoff to Gabe + Audimute price bump)

**Most recent shipped to PROD:** v1.39.0 вҖ” Marketing dashboard scaffolding (gated to Benton + Gabe ownerIds). Promoted 2026-05-22.

Today bundled three threads: (1) cleared yesterday's staging backlog with a five-version promote (v1.38.2 вҶ’ v1.39.0), (2) handed the marketing dashboard off to Gabe via a kick-off prompt вҖ” he turned around the Google Ads ETL implementation the same day (v1.40.0), (3) built out quote expiration indicators (v1.41.0) ahead of the Audimute price-book bump the user is rolling out today. Side detour into a HubSpot file-replacement lockout that turned out to be unrelated to our app. Full breakdown in the **May 22 session writeup** below.

**On STAGING (NOT YET promoted to main):**

- **v1.46.1** (2026-05-26, Gabe) вҖ” **Marketing вҖ” closed-loop attribution shipped + visual polish.** Two new endpoints in `marketing/router.js`: `/api/marketing/campaign-attribution` joins Google Ads campaigns вҶ” HubSpot contacts вҶ” HubSpot deals (first-touch via `first_converting_campaign` then `first_source_data_2`, filtered PAID_SEARCH/google), and `/api/marketing/attribution-coverage` returns the "trust thermometer" (% of recent closed-won deals + revenue + new contacts that are attributable). Campaign table on `marketing-dashboard.html` extended with four new columns (Leads / Deals / Revenue / True ROAS), True ROAS rendered as a color-coded pill (green вүҘ3x, yellow 1вҖ“3x, red <1x). New attribution coverage panel above the KPI strip вҖ” three stat blocks with progress bars (deals attributed, revenue attributed, contacts with source). Two new KPI cards (Closed Revenue, True ROAS) sit alongside the existing GA4-estimated value/ROAS so the user can directly compare "what GA4 thinks happened" vs "what HubSpot says actually happened." Single-touch first-touch attribution only (multi-touch would need full event/session history we don't pull); for apples-to-apples validation against HubSpot's Ads tool, set HubSpot to "First ad interaction" model. Also: per-bucket progress logging in `marketing/hubspot-etl.js` вҖ” each bucket completion now logs to console + writes intermediate `marketing_syncs` row, so the dashboard count climbs in real time during long syncs instead of staying frozen until the multi-hour sync finishes (addresses the v1.46.0 UX gap). Versioning: per the user's preference for the marketing module, this is a PATCH bump (1.46.0 вҶ’ 1.46.1) even though it adds features, overriding the CLAUDE.md "MINOR for features" rule while the dashboard is actively under construction.

- **v1.46.0** (2026-05-26, Gabe) вҖ” **Marketing вҖ” HubSpot sync date-bucketed for complete coverage.** v1.44.0 hit HubSpot's hard 10,000-result cap on the search API and silently truncated. Worse, the sort was ascending вҖ” so we kept the *oldest* 10k records and dropped the most-recently-modified ones (i.e. exactly the attribution-relevant ones). Found by querying HubSpot directly: WhisperRoom has ~26.6k contacts modified in the last year; we were getting 10k. Fix in `marketing/hubspot-etl.js`: split the 365-day lookback into 30-day buckets (12 per year) and run each as its own search query вҖ” each bucket has its own 10k headroom so coverage scales linearly. Sort within each bucket is now DESCENDING and buckets run newest-first, so the most useful data lands immediately even if the request times out partway through (the server keeps running after the browser gives up вҖ” observed in the v1.44.0 sync). Bucket errors don't abort the rest (partial coverage > none); first error + truncation warnings surface via `marketing_syncs.error`. Applies to both `syncHubSpotContacts` and `syncHubSpotDeals`. **Known unresolved:** the long sync still times out the frontend `fetch()` вҖ” needs a background-job pattern with polled status to actually fix the UX. Server-side completion is unaffected; data lands fine even when the browser shows "Failed to fetch".

- **v1.45.0** (2026-05-26, Benton) вҖ” **Reconcile: refunded deals + editable HubSpot popup.** Refund dealstage `895819` now included in the reconciler's HS deal filter; previously read-only HubSpot detail popup is now inline-editable for six properties with a Save button (PATCHes the deal in HubSpot via new `PATCH /api/reconcile/hs-deal/:dealId` endpoint).

- **v1.44.0** (2026-05-26, Gabe) вҖ” **Marketing dashboard вҖ” HubSpot ingestion (first leg of closed-loop attribution).** New `marketing/hubspot-etl.js` mirrors the Google Ads ETL pattern (envReady gate, per-runner error handling that writes to `marketing_syncs.error`, idempotent upserts). `syncHubSpotContacts` pulls contacts with gclid + first/latest-touch attribution pairs + lifecycle/lead-status (15 properties). `syncHubSpotDeals` pulls Sales-Pipeline deals only (`pipeline = "default"`; excludes the Test + Ecommerce pipelines), with stage, USD amount, close date, won/lost flags, days-to-close, and a denormalized `primary_contact_id` resolved via the v4 associations API. Incremental sync via `hs_lastmodifieddate` filter + cursor pagination; 365-day default lookback (vs Google Ads' 90 вҖ” deals need longer windows). Auth reuses the existing `HS_TOKEN` Railway env var; no new npm deps (Node built-in `https`, kept local to `marketing/` since the project rule forbids touching `lib/hubspot.js`). The existing `Sync All` button now refreshes everything (5 syncs total: 3 Google Ads + 2 HubSpot); explicit `hubspot_contacts` / `hubspot_deals` / `hubspot_all` report types available on `/api/marketing/sync` for targeted refresh. Status panel shows HubSpot sync state inline with Google Ads but does NOT block Sync All if `HS_TOKEN` is missing. **Not in this PR:** the attribution join table, any dashboard view changes, keyword/search-term-level attribution (needs `click_view` API resolution, deferred to a later PR). Plan: get raw HubSpot data flowing on staging first, eyeball it, then layer the attribution table on top.

- **v1.43.0** (2026-05-26, Gabe) вҖ” **Marketing dashboard вҖ” keyword + search-term aggregation views.** The two TODO stubs in `marketing-dashboard.html` (left over from v1.39.0 scaffolding) are now real tables. Keywords aggregate by `keyword_id` вҶ’ keyword text + match type + spend / clicks / CPC / conv / CPA. Search terms aggregate by normalized (lowercased + trimmed) search term вҶ’ term + same metrics minus match type. Both sort by spend descending; display capped to top 200 with the full row count shown in the section meta (a 90-day pull can yield thousands of distinct keywords, so capping keeps the page snappy). No ROAS column вҖ” Google Ads `conversion_value` is a campaign-level metric and isn't pulled by `keyword_view` or `search_term_view` reports. Stays staging-only (Test Sales Portal); not for `main` until the dashboard is genuinely useful and Benton signs off.

- **v1.42.2** (2026-05-22) вҖ” **DEVLOG: full session writeup for 2026-05-22.** Captured today's three threads (promote sweep, marketing handoff to Gabe + his v1.40.0/v1.42.1, expiration indicators v1.41.0) plus the HubSpot file-lockout side detour and the v1.42.0 marketing-open fix.

- **v1.42.1** (2026-05-22, Gabe) вҖ” **Marketing sync fixed: `google-ads-api` upgraded v17 вҶ’ v23.** Every sync (campaigns, keywords, search terms) failed with `12 UNIMPLEMENTED: GRPC target method can't be resolved`. Root cause: the pinned `google-ads-api@^17.0.0` targets a Google Ads API version Google has sunset, so gRPC calls had no live endpoint and died before reaching authentication вҖ” not an auth or credential problem. Benton approved the upgrade; `package.json` now pins `^23.0.0` (current latest). No change to `marketing/google-ads-etl.js` вҖ” `customer.report()` is stable across these versions. Watch on deploy: the Docker base is `node:18-slim` and v23 declares no `engines`, so npm won't block; if the build or sync throws a Node-version error, bump the base image to `node:20-slim`. After redeploy, re-run Sync All вҖ” calls will reach Google; next gate is developer-token access level (still Explorer; Basic Access application pending).

- **v1.42.0** (2026-05-22) вҖ” **Marketing dashboard opened to all reps (temporary).** Gabe was hitting an ownerId mismatch on the v1.40.0 allowlist вҖ” page kept redirecting him to /deals. Until that's diagnosed, `MARKETING_ALLOWLIST` in `marketing/router.js` is set to `[]` (empty array short-circuits the check to "any authenticated user"). Nav link in the Deal Hub topbar now shows for everyone (was gated client-side to Benton + Gabe). Re-gating is one edit вҖ” populate the array. User confirmed marketing page is working for Gabe after this change.

- **v1.41.0** (2026-05-22) вҖ” **Quote expiration indicators across Deal Hub + Quote Builder.** Yellow chip "EXP Nd" in last 7 days; red "EXPIRED" after 30 days. Driven by `quotes.created_at` (30-day rule matches the PDF footer). Shown on: (a) right-panel quote cards in Deal Hub, (b) deal cards on the main board (suppressed once deal is accepted/paid/has payment type вҖ” already locked in). Quote builder shows a dismissable banner on load when an expired/expiring quote opens. Accepted quotes never trigger the chip/banner. Server side: added `created_at` to `/api/deals/:id/hub` quotes array and `/api/quote-snapshot/`; `/api/history` injects `_createdAt` onto each snapshot row. **Not yet visually verified on staging** вҖ” user logged off before testing the chips/banner against a real expired quote.

- **v1.40.0** (2026-05-22) вҖ” **Marketing Google Ads sync implemented (Gabe, in his own session).** All three runners in `marketing/google-ads-etl.js` (`syncCampaigns`, `syncKeywords`, `syncSearchTerms`) are no longer stubs. `_getCustomer()` now builds the real `google-ads-api` client from the `GOOGLE_ADS_*` Railway env vars. Each runner pulls a daily-segmented report for the last N days (default 90) вҖ” `campaign` / `keyword_view` / `search_term_view` вҖ” and upserts into its `marketing_*` table on the composite PK, so re-runs overwrite cleanly. Google Ads API errors are caught per-runner and written to `marketing_syncs.error` so the dashboard status bar surfaces them. User mentioned Gabe pushed "something that affected the library" during the session вҖ” worth a quick `git log` review next session, but marketing page is functional now.

- **Supplier-spend drilldown deep links вҖ” verify QB txn-id mapping.** The "Open вҶ—" link on each row relies on QB exposing the underlying transaction id on one of the `ColData[i].id` cells. My flatten picks the first non-account id. If any row shows a dash in the QB column instead of "Open вҶ—", paste the row's type + doc # and we adjust the extraction.

- **HubSpot workflow rewrite вҖ” validate next fresh Shopify order.** Today's rewrite changes parts-order deals to TRANSITION (not duplicate) into the Sales Pipeline, preserving tax_price / source store / line items / contact assoc from the original Shopify-synced deal. Next live parts order tells us whether the data actually flows through. Old duplicate deals from the prior workflow are still orphaned in HubSpot вҖ” possible cleanup later.

- **Shopify API authentication вҖ” tabled.** Explored at length today. Conclusion: the new Shopify Dev Dashboard does not offer a static `shpat_` token for custom-distribution apps without standing up an OAuth callback handler (~30 min of work). Decision was to stick with HubSpot-mirror data for the Shopify-parts auto-invoice for now. If precision tax / address / line items become a real pain point, options are (a) install Intuit's official ShopifyвҶ’QB integration and let it own all ShopifyвҶ’QB sync, or (b) build the OAuth callback. See May 20 writeup В§6 for the trail.

- **Email-reply logs v2 вҖ” feedback capture.** Deliberately not in v1. Revisit once there's enough history in the `email_reply_logs` table to make manual review valuable. Likely shape: thumbs up/down + an "edited final" textarea that captures what the rep actually sent (if different from what the model produced), so we can build a dataset of "model output вҶ’ human-corrected output" pairs.

### TaxJar compliance investigation (TABLED вҖ” keeping notes for future reference)

v1.22.0 (TaxJar line-item mode) and v1.22.1 (manual FL В§212.054 surtax cap) were reverted from staging on 2026-05-18 вҖ” user chose to table the entire workstream. The reverts preserve the code in git history, so the work can be resurrected by reverting the revert commits when ready. What surfaced before tabling:

- TaxJar's `/v2/taxes` endpoint **does not auto-apply state-specific per-item caps** вҖ” confirmed for FL even in line-item mode. Likely also misses TN single-article cap, MA $175 clothing, etc.
- User confirmed TaxJar's AutoFile **files on its own calculated number, NOT on what was actually collected via Shopify/QB**. Dashboard shows "what we collected" vs. "what we should have collected" vs. "discrepancy" вҖ” and files the higher (TaxJar-calculated) number.
- Mechanism of leak: QB AST + Shopify both correctly apply state caps at invoice time вҶ’ customer pays the correct (lower) amount вҶ’ TaxJar's records say "should have collected $X" using uncapped flat rate вҶ’ TaxJar files $X вҶ’ WhisperRoom remits the gap out of pocket.
- User mentioned a TN incident a few months back where Shopify charged "less than what the total tax rate was" and TaxJar then "filed that we owed more money to the government." That's a concrete confirmation this isn't theoretical.
- Per-order amounts are small (FL = ~1% Г— amount-over-$5k-cap, so ~$7 on the Pinellas booth) but it's compounding silently across years and multiple states.

If/when picked back up: items worth revisiting include emailing TaxJar support on AutoFile actuals-vs-calculated, pulling historical FL orders to verify the leak is recurring, the reconciliation script (Closed Won vs QB `TxnTaxDetail.TotalTax` vs TaxJar-would-have-filed), nexus list verification (`lib/states.js:8-25` has 16 states; user thought 14), and the strategic stay/Stripe-Tax/Avalara decision. Process-side: add CPA-level human review of monthly filings regardless of software choice.

- **v1.21.10** (this session, May 15 PM) вҖ” User raised the question: when an order is processed, is the correct freight amount actually transferred to HubSpot's `freight_cost` deal field? Trace found three connected bugs:
  - `/api/process-order` closedwon PATCH was missing amount/tax_rate/freight_cost/discount entirely. The Freight LINE ITEM got rebuilt on the deal but `freight_cost` (the deal property) was never patched. So if the rep edited freight after quote creation, HubSpot kept the original value.
  - `/api/create-deal` open-stage path (`dealPatchProps` around quote-server.js:2902) had amount/tax_rate/total_tax_amount/discount but was missing freight_cost. So updating a quote on an open deal silently failed to push freight.
  - `/api/create-deal` locked-stage path (quote-server.js:2856-2900): the May 13 carve-out that financial-PATCHed closed deals on every new quote creation was overreaching вҖ” Merge Deal (/api/deals/:id/merge) and Modify Order (/api/orders/:q/add-charge) each have their own endpoints and don't go through /api/create-deal. So the locked-stage patch was firing on ANY new quote creation against a closed deal, silently rewriting its financials. Per user's clarified rule ("unless the order is closed, it should be updating; closed = read-only except for the explicit Modify Order action"), the locked-stage branch is now a no-op log.
  - Net behavior: open deals get full financial sync on create/update; process-order does the FINAL sync as the deal transitions to closedwon; closed deals are read-only from /api/create-deal thereafter (use Modify Order for changes).

- **v1.21.0** (this session, May 15) вҖ” Shopify Orders drawer + 60s auto-refresh. New рҹӣ’ button in Deal Hub topbar opens a right-side slide-out drawer listing every ecommerce-owned deal in three sections: Awaiting Verification (вүҘ$5k, no quote yet вҖ” orange chip, the booth orders Jill needs to verify), Small Orders (under $5k, no quote yet вҖ” parts orders for spot-checking), In Progress (already has a quote in our system). Button glows orange with a pulse when there are pending verifications; neutral count badge otherwise. Polls every 60s. Click any row вҶ’ existing deal hub overlay вҶ’ "+ New Quote" вҶ’ normal quote flow. Ecommerce-owned deals now EXCLUDED from main `/api/deals/list` results вҖ” drawer is their home, also sidesteps the HubSpot search quirk from yesterday. Deal Hub board itself also auto-refreshes every 60s now (matches admin-log polling pattern). Two new env-overridable constants: `ECOMMERCE_OWNER_ID` (default 49384873) and `SHOPIFY_VERIFY_THRESHOLD` (default $5000). New endpoint `GET /api/shopify-pending`.

Today's progression (May 14, in order):

- **v1.20.7** вҖ” accept ACH + wire alongside card. Per-quote `allowCC` / `allowACH` / `allowWire` checkboxes in both Create Invoice modals (quote builder + deal hub), all default ON. `lib/stripe.js` builds `payment_settings.payment_method_types` dynamically; when wire is on, adds the required `customer_balance.bank_transfer.type: us_bank_transfer`. Days-until-due stretches 7 вҶ’ 14 when ACH on so legit payers don't see "past due" before ACH clears. Defensive: wire silently drops (`stripe.invoice.wire-dropped` log) if customer has no name. Use case: uncheck CC on $50k+ orders to skip 3.4% fee. Stripe Dashboard ACH + Bank Transfers confirmed enabled in test mode.

- **v1.20.8** вҖ” Deal Hub invoice rows reflect Stripe paid state. When `json_snapshot.stripe.status === 'paid'`, the deal-hub response overlays `status='paid'` + `paidVia='stripe'` + `stripeInvoiceId` + `stripeDashboardUrl` onto the HubSpot-sourced row. UI renders a purple "Stripe" badge + "Stripe вҶ—" link jumping to the Stripe Dashboard. Existing /admin-log toggle gates the overlay вҖ” flipping OFF makes the server skip Stripe entirely.

- **v1.20.9** вҖ” **critical fix.** Stripe webhook had been returning 401 to EVERY delivery since v1.20.0 shipped (8+ days). The global auth middleware at `quote-server.js:564` rejects `/api/*` requests without a session cookie, and `/api/stripe/webhook` wasn't in the `isPublicRoute` allowlist. Stripe authenticates via signed body, not cookies. So every webhook attempt bounced off auth before our handler ran вҖ” zero `invoice.paid` events processed for the entire integration period. Caught by inspecting Stripe Workbench вҶ’ Webhooks вҶ’ Event deliveries (saw 9+ `401 ERR` attempts). One-line fix: added webhook path to the allowlist. Signature verification in the handler is preserved (only requests with valid `Stripe-Signature` get processed). Stripe auto-retried queued events over the next hour and they all landed.

- **v1.20.10** вҖ” two workflow upgrades hanging off `invoice.paid` (now working): (1) **Deal cards turn green** when an invoice is paid (Stripe-paid via toggle-gated snapshot flag OR HubSpot `payment_status='paid'`), in addition to existing quote-accepted/payment-type triggers. (2) **Auto-advance HubSpot deal stage** to "Verbal Confirmation" (`contractsent`) on `invoice.paid` webhook, but ONLY if currently at an earlier stage. Skips `contractsent`/`closedwon`/`845719`/`closedlost` to never walk a deal backwards. New log events: `stripe.deal-stage-advanced`, `stripe.deal-stage-noop`, `error.stripe.deal-stage`.

- **v1.20.11 вҶ’ v1.20.12 (reverted)** вҖ” added a dedicated Shipped-stage catch-all pass mirroring Closed Won. Brought in more old Shipped deals as expected, but did NOT solve the immediate problem (a brand-new Shopify deal was missing from the board). Reverted to keep the board clean while we investigate.

**Diagnostic endpoints added today (no version bump, debug-only):**
- `GET /api/debug/deal/:id` вҖ” fetches raw HubSpot deal properties + the pipeline definition (with all stage IDs вҶ” labels). Used to verify a deal's actual internal `dealstage`/`pipeline` vs. what we filter on.
- `GET /api/debug/find-deal?q=...` вҖ” searches HubSpot deals by name and returns up to 20 matches with IDs and key properties.

### Open investigation: Shopify deals invisible from Deal Hub [RESOLVED 2026-05-20]

The HubSpot workflow rewrite (transition the original Shopify-synced deal into the Sales Pipeline instead of creating a duplicate) sidesteps this entirely вҖ” the source-of-truth deal is now in the pipeline our app reads, complete with the Shopify-synced data. The HubSpot search-index quirk no longer matters. Keeping the notes below for historical context.

---

Late EOD May 14 we hit a real bug we couldn't fully diagnose. Two newly-arrived Shopify-generated deals вҖ” IDs `60254716188` (#2144, $5,046.50) and `60256150594` (#2145, $11,180.80) вҖ” landed in HubSpot's Sales Pipeline at stage `845719` (Shipped) with owner `49384873` (ecommerce@whisperroom.com). Both are missing from the Deal Hub board.

**What we ruled out:**
- Pipeline mismatch вҖ” confirmed in Sales Pipeline (`default`), confirmed stage is genuinely `845719` (not a duplicate-named stage), pipeline definition verified via `/api/debug/deal/:id`
- Rep filter вҖ” user verified "All Reps" was selected
- "Hide HubSpot Only" toggle вҖ” verified off
- Pagination depth вҖ” added dedicated Shipped catch-all in v1.20.11 (brought in MORE old Shipped deals), didn't surface these
- These deals ARE returned by `/api/deals/list?stage=845719&limit=500` (explicitly filtering to Shipped) вҖ” verified by Ctrl+F on deal ID
- These deals ARE returned by `/api/debug/find-deal?q=Shopify+%232144` вҖ” HubSpot's text-search index has them

**The leading suspect:** something about how HubSpot's deal-search API handles deals owned by `49384873` (ecommerce service user) in combination with the `dealstage IN [5 stages]` filter we use on the default load. Single-stage filter (`?stage=845719`) returns them; multi-stage filter does not. Probably a HubSpot search-index quirk specific to that owner ID or to the way Shopify deals are tagged.

User comment from EOD: "I have to specifically search '2145'. If I type shopify, lots comes up, but definitely not the most recent ones we sold." So even the text-search has weirdness вҖ” older Shopify deals match the search, the most recent ones don't unless you search by their specific number.

**Decision (user-driven):** rather than chase down the HubSpot search quirk, build a new **"Shopify Review" column** in the Deal Hub that pulls ALL ecommerce-owned deals (`ownerId === '49384873'`) regardless of HubSpot stage. This sidesteps the search bug AND fixes a real workflow gap (the HubSpot Shopify integration auto-advances new Shopify deals to "Shipped" stage on creation, which is correct for small parts orders but WRONG for booth orders that need human verification before processing).

### Queued (next session): build "Shopify Review" column [SUPERSEDED 2026-05-20]

User opted for a different approach: rewrite the upstream HubSpot workflow to TRANSITION the original Shopify-synced deal into the Sales Pipeline (booth orders вҶ’ Verbal Confirmation stage; parts orders stay in Order Pipeline owned by ecommerce). That obviates the need for a separate "Shopify Review" column. Notes below retained as historical context.

---

**The workflow problem:** Shopify orders auto-create HubSpot deals via a workflow that drops them in "Shipped" (presumably because Shopify already collected payment + the small parts orders ship automatically from the Shopify side). But booth orders ($5k+) come through the same Shopify checkout and end up in the same "Shipped" stage вҖ” which is wrong because they haven't been verified, quoted, or processed by sales. Jill needs to contact the customer, confirm what they're getting + shipping, then create a real quote and process it like a normal order.

**Two paths to fix (not mutually exclusive):**

- **Path A вҖ” Fix the HubSpot workflow at the source:** change the auto-advance logic to put deals over $X into a different stage (or new "Shopify Review" stage). No-code change inside HubSpot Workflows. Cleanest long-term answer. We aren't doing this in next session unless user wants to.
- **Path B вҖ” Build a "Shopify Review" column in our Deal Hub:** **THIS IS THE PLAN.** Column criteria: `ownerId === '49384873'`, regardless of HubSpot stage. Effectively removes ecommerce deals from the Shipped column and gives them their own home. Doesn't touch the HubSpot workflow (no risk of breaking the small-parts auto-flow).

**Sketch for the column (locked decisions from EOD May 14 discussion):**
- Column shows ALL ecommerce-owned deals (not just $5k+), so small parts orders are visible too вҖ” Jill can spot-check anything weird
- Card displays an orange `Booth вҖ” Verify` chip if `amount >= $5000`, no chip otherwise вҖ” visual priority signal
- Click вҶ’ existing deal hub overlay вҶ’ existing "+ New Quote" button. Jill builds a real quote bound to the Shopify-created deal, sends to customer, processes like normal.
- Deal LEAVES the Shopify Review column once `latestQuote` is set on it (sales has created a real quote вҖ” deal now flows through normal columns based on actual stage)

**Three scoping questions still unanswered (ask user first thing next session):**
1. Threshold for "Booth вҖ” Verify" chip вҖ” $5k as proposed, or different?
2. Show all Shopify deals in column, or only ones above some amount? (Recommended: all, only big ones get the chip.)
3. When Jill creates a quote against a Shopify deal, should it move out of the column entirely (recommended) or stay with a "Quote Sent" indicator?

**Estimated effort:** ~half-day. New COLUMNS entry in `deals-dashboard.html`, server-side `shopifyReview` flag in `/api/deals/list` based on ownerId, exclude these deals from the Shipped column (so they only appear in Shopify Review). Bonus: ALSO fixes the visibility bug we couldn't track down вҖ” these deals will appear in their own column whether or not HubSpot's search index includes them in default queries.

Yesterday's progression (May 13):

- **v1.20.6** вҖ” switched the discount display from per-line baking (v1.20.5) to a native Stripe Coupon attached to the invoice via `discounts[]`. Hosted invoice now shows a single "Discount" row under the subtotal вҖ” the standard B2B-invoice convention. Freight/tax/install invoiceitems flagged `discountable:false` so the coupon only hits product lines (matches HubSpot's `hs_discount_percentage` scope). Coupon is created one-shot per invoice (`duration:once`, `max_redemptions:1`) and named "N% Off вҖ” Quote W-XXX" so it's traceable in the Stripe dashboard. `previewTotalCents` reworked to mirror Stripe's aggregate-then-round math so it matches `amount_due` to the cent. Also polish: friendly `footer` ("Thank you for choosing WhisperRoomвҖҰ"), and `custom_fields` for Quote Number + Deal ID so support can cross-reference from Stripe. Logo/brand color/business name are configured separately in Stripe Dashboard вҶ’ Settings вҶ’ Branding (one-time, no code) and propagate to all hosted invoices automatically.
- **v1.20.5** вҖ” wired the quote-level discount into Stripe. HubSpot's path was passing `hs_discount_percentage` per line; Stripe has no equivalent field, so the discount silently dropped (Stripe total = gross instead of net). `lib/stripe.js` now bakes `item.lineDiscount` into each line's cents amount and appends "(N% off, was $X)" to the description so the customer sees the discount on the hosted page. Freight/tax/install lines carry `lineDiscount=0` already, so the discount stays product-only just like HubSpot. `previewTotalCents` in `/api/create-invoice` updated to apply the same math so the fail-loud guard does not misfire and the success-log preview matches Stripe's finalized `amount_due`.
- **v1.20.4** вҖ” fixed the doubling bug introduced by v1.20.3's first real test. v1.20.3's `pending_invoice_items_behavior: include` correctly attached the new items but ALSO swept in every orphan pending invoiceitem the customer had accumulated from pre-v1.20.3 failed runs вҖ” so the invoice was ~2Г— expected. Switched to draft-first, attach-directly: create the empty invoice draft, then create each `/v1/invoiceitems` with `invoice: draft.id`. No pending-bucket interaction means orphan items from any past or future failed run cannot contaminate. `pending_invoice_items_behavior: exclude` set explicitly as belt-and-suspenders. Stale pending invoiceitems on the test customers from yesterday's runs are still in Stripe sandbox but no longer harmful вҖ” clean up via Stripe dashboard (test mode вҶ’ Customers вҶ’ delete pending invoiceitems, or delete the customers entirely).
- **v1.20.3** вҖ” fixed the $0-invoice bug from today's first real rep-flow test. Root cause: `lib/stripe.js` was POSTing `/v1/invoices` without `pending_invoice_items_behavior: include`. Stripe's API default flipped from `include` to `exclude` in version 2022-11-15, so the freshly-created `/v1/invoiceitems` (pending) never attached to the new draft вҶ’ draft finalized at $0 вҶ’ hosted invoice page reads "already paid." The existing `/api/debug/stripe-diagnostic` route already had the flag (`quote-server.js:841`), which is why the May 12 diagnostic ran clean end-to-end at $4716.40 but today's real rep-flow attempt produced a $0 invoice. Also added a fail-loud guard: `createInvoiceForQuote` now takes `expectedTotalCents` from the caller and throws if Stripe returns `amount_due=0` when we expected positive. `/api/create-invoice` passes `previewTotalCents` through. The error surfaces as `error.stripe.invoice` in `/admin-log` instead of a silent $0 success.

- **v1.20.0** вҖ” first cut. `lib/stripe.js` new module. `/api/create-invoice` creates Stripe Invoice alongside HubSpot's. `/i/:quoteNumber` Pay Now prefers Stripe `hosted_invoice_url`. Webhook handler with signature verification. Canadian orders skipped. Stripe state on `json_snapshot.stripe` (no schema migration). Hard-locked to `sk_test_` keys.
- **v1.20.1** вҖ” fixed two bugs found on first test: (1) Stripe `/v1/invoiceitems` rejected `price_data.product_data` (that's a Checkout Sessions field, not Invoice Items). Switched to simpler `amount` + `description` (qty pre-multiplied into cents; qty prefix baked into description so customer still sees "2 Г— Foo"). (2) `customer.email` was missing on `/api/create-invoice` body вҖ” added cascading fallback: body вҶ’ `json_snapshot.customer.email` вҶ’ HubSpot contact lookup via `resolvedContactId`. `emailSource` logged in success meta.
- **v1.20.2** вҖ” toggle + $0 safety. (1) New ON/OFF toggle pill in `/admin-log` topbar, backed by `kv_store.stripe_enabled`. When OFF, BOTH new invoice creation AND existing invoice page Pay Now fall back to HubSpot. Webhook still processes events. Endpoints: `GET/POST /api/stripe-toggle`. 10s memory cache. (2) `$0-total guard` вҖ” Stripe finalizes $0 invoices as immediately PAID, which is what produced today's "already paid" report. Now if `invoiceLineItems` positives sum to вүӨ$0, skip Stripe creation with a `stripe.invoice.skipped` log including line counts. (3) Diagnostics: `stripe.invoice.created` meta now carries `lineItemCount`, `positiveItemCount`, `previewTotalCents`, `emailSource`.

**Stripe diagnostic endpoints** (kept from May 12): `/api/debug/stripe-diagnostic` + `/api/debug/stripe-cleanup` вҖ” useful for one-off testing outside the rep flow.

**Queued (per May 14 ship-to-process discussion):**

- **Embedded Payment Element on /i/ вҖ” explicitly DEFERRED** (Option B from May 13 discussion). User decided May 14 to stick with the redirect-to-Stripe-hosted flow for now. Reasoning: customers don't perceive the redirect as friction the way developers do, and embedded would mean rebuilding Stripe's hosted-page UX (already-paid state, decline retries, 3DS challenge, ACH processing state UI, wire funding-instructions display). Total cost: card-only embedded ~1 day, +ACH ~2 days, +wire ~3-4 days. Re-evaluate after 1-2 weeks of real customer use if anyone balks at the redirect.

- **Order-processing settlement policy (May 14 decision):** payment method dictates how long to hold before shipping.
  - **Wire** (`customer_balance`): clears in 1вҖ“2 business days; **effectively irreversible** once received. Process on `invoice.paid`. Safe.
  - **Card**: clears instantly; chargeback window is 120 days (Visa/MC) but practical risk is 30вҖ“60 days. Process on `invoice.paid` for normal orders. Keep signed BOL + order acceptance as chargeback evidence.
  - **ACH**: clears in 4вҖ“5 business days; **reversal window is 60 days** for "unauthorized" reasons. Process on `invoice.paid` for established customers. For **first-time customer + large order ($5k+)**, hold 7 days after `paid` as a fraud margin.
  - Stripe webhook fires `invoice.paid` ONLY after bank-network clearing for ACH/wire (not on initial submit) вҖ” so the webhook is a real "money has settled to Stripe" signal, not a "customer hit submit" signal.

- **ACH `processing` status follow-up** (deferred вҖ” would be nice not urgent): Between customer-submits-ACH (day 0) and `paid` (day 4вҖ“5), Stripe's `payment_intent.status` is `processing`. We don't currently surface this in `/admin-log` or anywhere rep-facing. Means an ACH-in-flight order is invisible to reps during the gap. Worth adding a `stripe.invoice.processing` log event (subscribed via webhook) + maybe a "ACH pending" badge on the deal hub once enough orders flow through to justify the UI.

- **Cross-system "paid" sync** (deferred вҖ” same as yesterday): on `invoice.paid` from Stripe, also patch the HubSpot invoice to paid so reconciliation isn't manual. Not urgent during the observation period since HubSpot AR aging reads deal amounts, not invoice paid-state.

- **New-customer-ACH hold automation** (deferred): rep-side notification when a $5k+ ACH payment comes from a first-time customer, so the rep can verify before shipping. Nice-to-have once we see real volume.

- **Auto-suppress CC above $X threshold** (deferred): currently the rep manually unchecks the CC box on $50k+ orders. Could auto-uncheck-and-warn at $50k. Low priority since the $50k warning banner already nudges the rep.

---

**Open questions / things to investigate next session:**
- The "already paid $0 invoice" symptom from today should be fixed by v1.20.2's guard вҖ” but worth tracing WHY a quote ended up with $0 total. Likely freight-only or pickup-only quote (no product lines). The `stripe.invoice.skipped` meta will now show `lineItemCount` so we can confirm.
- Verify `STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET` is set. If you trigger a real test payment and `/admin-log` shows no `stripe.invoice-paid` event, the secret is the first suspect.
- Cross-system "paid" state: when a Stripe invoice gets paid, HubSpot's invoice for the same quote stays "unpaid" because we don't sync the state back. Need a follow-up: on `invoice.paid` webhook, also patch HubSpot's invoice to `paid` (or mark deal stage). Not urgent during observation, but list as follow-up.
- Quote loaded from history may not refresh `body.customer.email` cleanly вҖ” investigate the client path (probably quote-builder.html `loadFromHistoryEntry`) if email-fallback log meta keeps showing `emailSource: snapshot` or `hubspot-contact` instead of `body`. Not blocking but worth tightening.

**Roll-forward path when comfortable:** stagingвҶ’main merge via `/promote` will bring v1.19.18 (light-mode polish) + v1.20.0/1/2 (Stripe) to prod in one commit. Don't promote yet вҖ” let Stripe simmer on staging until 2-3 weeks of observation pass.

**Active theme:** Replace HubSpot customer-facing invoices with Stripe Invoices (Option 2 from the May 12 discussion). Option A is the lightest delivery of that vision вҖ” full Stripe Invoice exists in the background; customer just sees Stripe's hosted page instead of HubSpot's when they click Pay Now. Next phases once observation passes: (a) optional embedded Payment Element on `/i/` (so customers never leave our page), (b) Refund button in Order Hub, (c) eventually disable HubSpot invoice creation. HubSpot Payments is Stripe under the hood; `hs_fees_amount` IS Stripe's rate; `hs_platform_fee` (~0.5%) is HubSpot's markup we save going direct. ~$80 per $16k card transaction, $7-10k/year. Decisions locked from May 12: TaxJar stays, payment link goes in OUR email/PDF (`auto_advance: false`), no Stripe-side reminder emails, AR aging untouched.

**Outstanding work (not yet started):**

Especially **#1 (public endpoints lack share-token auth)** and **#2 (XSS in server-rendered HTML)** вҖ” both are exploitable by anonymous visitors.
- v1.11.0 promoted to main 2026-05-11. **v1.12.0 on staging вҖ” paused mid-feature, will resume later.** Spot-test the To/CC+ module on Process Order from both Deal Hub and Quote Builder, verify the recipients land in `order_data.shipEmailTo` / `order_data.shipEmailCc` and pre-populate the Orders drawer when the order is opened.

Needs them to specify which SKUs/booths are wrong; we update the map then. The shared computeShipmentEstimate helper (v1.9.6) makes this a one-place fix when ready. *(Update 2026-05-12: orders-dashboard's copy was synced to QB's in v1.12.4 вҖ” QB is the source of truth. ## Session writeup вҖ” June 5, 2026 (v1.66.2 вҶ’ v1.72.4 вҖ” Packing List generator + /weights tooling + Add/Duplicate Quote + QB Activity)

Big multi-thread day. **Two prod promotes:** `71ddd67` (mid-day: /weights + PL generator + QB Activity + Drive PDF fix + weight corrections) and `75306dc` (Add Pallet + marketing). Gabe shipped marketing GSC/SEO/Growth-Engine work in parallel all day, so nearly every push collided on the shared `package.json`/changelog/DEVLOG вҖ” handled by rebase + renumber each time (the package.json detangling in `project_gabe_scope` would end this).

- Built the hidden **`/weights`** reconciliation page (v1.67.0): per-MDL net (PL BOM) вҶ’ pallets вҶ’ gross (net + palletsГ—144) вҶ’ HubSpot price-book weight вҶ’ О”. NV variants inherit pallet count (SNVвҶ’S/ENVвҶ’E) (v1.67.2). Refreshed with the **rounded re-pull** of all 104 base PLs (v1.67.3; `lib/model-weights.json`, all nets whole-integer). Added **Net/Pallet column** vs 1800-lb max with reduce hints (v1.69.2) and **click-to-expand per-pallet dimensions** (v1.70.1, from `BOOTH_DATA` вҶ’ `lib/pl-data/pallet-dims.json`).
- Fixed a **latent freight bug**: 102168/102186 were missing from `PALLETS_PER_MDL` (under-counted pallets in process-order) (v1.67.4). Refreshed corrected PLs as Benton fixed them (96192 NV, 102186 ENV, 102168 SNV/ENV).

**Thread 2 вҖ” PL data foundation (Phase 0, complete & reconciled).** Re-extracted `base_bom.json` (rounded). **Built `components-master.json` from the workbook `Parts` sheet** (1036 parts вҖ” had to bypass `extract_pl.py`'s 500-row cap by reading the sheet directly). **Validation: 104/104 base BOMs fully resolve, 0 weight mismatches** вҖ” ОЈ(component lbГ—qty) reproduces every model's net. Slimmed into `lib/pl-data/base-bom.json` + `components-master.json`.

**Thread 3 вҖ” PL generator Phase 1 spine (v1.69.0, LIVE).** `lib/packing-list.js` `generate(lineItems)` вҶ’ rooms (MDL-boundary parse) вҶ’ booth BOM вҶ’ `GET /pl/:quoteNumber` + `packing-list.html` viewer (per-room tables, exact weights, hinge/foam header defaults, editable qty/add/remove, **optional features flagged not applied**). "View Packing List" button by Build Assembly Manual. **Started feature-rule derivation** from the 5 example PLs (their headers list the features!): **EFSвҶ’+F03Г—vents, VSSвҶ’+F02Г—vents, MJPвҶ’+F09 confirmed**; DESK/SL/ADA/windows deferred. **Findings:** hinge/foam header fields are mostly notes BUT **hinge is actually a component swap** (door/opening codes flip by hand); features scale with vent count / booth size; windows aren't always in the header.

**Thread 4 вҖ” Quote Builder features.** **Duplicate Quote** (v1.71.0): search any past quote (customer/deal/#) вҶ’ copy its line items in вҶ’ re-verify prices; reuses `/api/history`, products-only. Moved its button into the Customer Info header (v1.71.1). **+ Add Pallet** (v1.72.0, default 90Г—47Г—40 in v1.72.1): manual pallets for loose components; centralized all pallet math into `getQuotePallets()` so extras flow into the freight quote (weight redistributes), weight box, intl request, snapshot, and order pallet count.

(Gabe later enriched it to v1.70.0.)

**Thread 6 вҖ” Drive PDF crash fix (v1.67.5).** Reps hit "Failed to launch the browser process вҖҰ posix_spawn chrome_crashpad_handler: Resource temporarily unavailable" on Drive uploads. Root cause: the freight tracking poller launched a **second, uncoordinated Chromium** outside pdf.js's single-flight semaphore. Fix: shared `pdf.withBrowser()` вҖ” **only one Chromium app-wide now** (saved `project_single_chromium_rule`).

**Thread 7 вҖ” Pallet-reduction pass (v1.72.4, in progress).** Benton is lowering pallet counts on large booths to cut LTL handling units. Did 102168/102186/96192 (5вҶ’4), 102168 S/102186 S (3вҶ’2), 10284 (3вҶ’2, then rebalanced), 102126 footprint. Touches `BOOTH_DATA` + `PALLETS_PER_MDL` + regenerated `pallet-dims.json`. ## Session writeup вҖ” May 22, 2026 (promote sweep + v1.40.0 Gabe + v1.41.0 + v1.42.0)

Shorter day than yesterday's marathon. Three workstreams plus an unrelated HubSpot rabbit hole.

### 1. Promote sweep (cleared yesterday's backlog)

Started the day promoting **v1.38.2 вҶ’ v1.39.0** to main in one merge вҖ” five versions sitting on staging covering AP PO lifecycle (auto-status + tracking widget + Jill/Benton notifications), overdue-ship-date sweep, editable freight quote ref on the order drawer, TaxJar ZIP-rejection fallback fix, and the marketing dashboard scaffolding. Merge commit `18c4f5a`. After this, main is on v1.39.0.

### 2. Marketing dashboard handoff to Gabe вҖ” and Gabe's same-day v1.40.0

Wrote a self-contained kick-off prompt for Gabe to paste into a fresh Claude Code session. Included: repo URL pointing to `staging/marketing` (since `main` didn't have the folder yet at write time), required reading order (CLAUDE.md вҶ’ DEVLOG вҶ’ his ETL file вҶ’ HANDOFF.md), hard constraints (only edit `marketing/` + `marketing-dashboard.html`, same Postgres with `marketing_` prefix, all work on staging), architecture overview, and the env-var bootstrap sequence (developer token вҶ’ OAuth client id/secret вҶ’ refresh token вҶ’ customer id вҶ’ optional login customer id).

Gabe came back same-day with **v1.40.0** вҖ” wired all three ETL runners (`syncCampaigns`, `syncKeywords`, `syncSearchTerms`) to the `google-ads-api` client, each pulling a daily-segmented report and upserting into the corresponding `marketing_*` table on the composite PK. API errors recorded to `marketing_syncs.error` so the dashboard status bar surfaces them instead of bare 500s. Push collided with my in-progress v1.40.0 (expiration indicators) вҖ” rebased my work to **v1.41.0** to resolve the version clash. User mentioned in passing that Gabe pushed something that "affected the library" вҖ” unclear what that meant in context; marketing page works now and we'll dig in next session if anything else is amiss.

### 3. Quote expiration indicators (v1.41.0)

User's framing: Audimute is bumping prices, and existing quotes need to stay at their original pricing for the 30 days they were valid for. After that, any quote going out needs to reflect new pricing. So the ask was a visual nudge for reps вҖ” not a notification (rep explicitly said that would be too noisy) вҖ” to refresh expired/expiring quotes before sending.

Three pieces built in concert:

- **Quote card chip** (Deal Hub right panel, quotes list): yellow `EXP Nd` chip (countdown of days left) when within 7 days of the 30-day window, red `EXPIRED` chip past 30. Sits next to existing RM/CUST/AP chips. Suppressed for accepted quotes вҖ” pricing was committed when the customer signed.

- **Deal card chip** (Deal Hub board): same yellow/red badge driven by `lastQuoteAt` (already on the deal-list response). Suppressed for deals already in a "green" state вҖ” accepted, paid, payment-type set. Locked-in deals stay clean.

- **Quote builder banner**: dismissable amber/red banner at the top of the page when an existing quote with age > 23 days is loaded. Wired into `loadFromHistoryEntry()` so it triggers regardless of entry path (URL param, history-panel click, Deal Hub click). Accepted quotes skip the banner.

Server side, exposed `created_at` (or its surrogates `createdAt` / `_createdAt`) on three endpoints so the client could compute expiration without a second fetch per quote: `/api/deals/:id/hub` (quotes array), `/api/quote-snapshot/:q` (top-level), `/api/history` (injected onto each snapshot via `{ ...r.json_snapshot, _createdAt: r.created_at }`). All driven off the canonical `quotes.created_at` DB column вҖ” matches the "Valid for 30 days" footer baked into the PDF.

EOD note: the indicators are deployed to staging but **not yet visually verified** вҖ” user logged off before opening a >30-day-old quote to confirm the chip + banner render. Fast to validate next session.

### 4. HubSpot file-replacement lockout (unrelated, no code change)

User hit a HubSpot UI problem unrelated to our app: trying to replace the Assembly Manual PDF in Content > Files, the Replace button was grayed out with "Files used in quotes cannot be replaced." Spent time diagnosing вҖ” turned out one of his old test quotes (from before the switch to our custom builder) was accepted, and HubSpot won't let you delete accepted quotes or detach files from them. Even archiving doesn't release the lock; archive вү  delete in HubSpot's lock check. Confirmed templates wouldn't help either (lock message specifically says "quotes," and once a template is used to create a quote, the quote owns its own copy of references).

User chose the workaround: uploaded the new manual as a new file (HubSpot gives a new URL) and updated all the places his app references the URL. Frustrating but reversible. The cleaner exit was HubSpot Support вҶ’ force-delete the accepted quote, but the URL-swap took less time than that conversation would have.

### 5. Marketing dashboard opened to all reps (v1.42.0)

Late-day fire. Gabe couldn't get into `/marketing` even after his v1.40.0 was live вҖ” server kept redirecting him to `/deals`. The v1.39.0 allowlist gates on `session.ownerId === '36303670' || '36320208'`. His session probably never hydrated his ownerId (we have the lazy-hydration code from v1.37.2/v1.37.4/v1.37.11 but it might not have fired for him), or his actual ownerId differs from what we put in the list.

Quick fix: emptied `MARKETING_ALLOWLIST` to `[]` and made `isAllowed()` treat that as "any authenticated user." Also un-gated the nav link in the Deal Hub topbar (was hidden behind an inline `MARKETING_OWNERS = ['36303670', '36320208']` check in `loadCurrentUser()` вҖ” removed). User confirmed marketing is now working for Gabe.

Re-locking is a one-line edit once we diagnose the mismatch: populate the array back in `marketing/router.js`. Worth doing вҖ” the marketing data isn't something we want every rep poking at.
